# Changelog

All notable changes to LogYourBody will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to Calendar-based [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

Version format: YYYY.MM.PATCH
- YYYY: Current year
- MM: Current month (01-12)
- PATCH: Incremental number for releases within the same month
